1b1(mdo): rgyag skad du/ yAr+yAg+h+rA byA ha na ma ma hA yAn sdung / bod skad du/ 
1b2(mdo): 'phags pa rgyan stug po bkod pa zhes bya ba theg pa chen po'i mdo/ bam po dang po/ sangs
1b3(mdo): rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag gis thos pa
1b4(mdo): dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das chos thams cad la mnga' sbyar ba 'dod pa nas/ gzugs
1b5(mdo): dang / gzugs med pa dang / gzugs med pa'i sems can rnams las 'das te
2a1(mdo): sangs rgyas kyi zhing stug po na stobs mnga' ba rnams dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams kyis/ 
2a2(mdo): rnam par 'phrul zhing rjes su spyod pa/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnal 'byor dam pa'i rnal 'byor
2a3(mdo): can 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po mur 'dug byed pa thams cad kyi gzhung rnam par 'angom
2a4(mdo): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po blo gros chen po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa'
2a5(mdo): chen po sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad kyi rnam par dgod pa yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du ston pa dang / byang chub sem
2a6(mdo): dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen
2b1(mdo): khyen po brnyam pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnam par 'phrul pa'i rgyal po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa can po 'jam dpal gnon dur gyur pa dang / byang // 
2b2(mdo): tul sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnam par grol ba'i zla ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shugs 'dzin da
2b3(mdo): de dag la sogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi ning bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba bye ba snyed kyi/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po khams gsum pa'i yul la sa yongs su 'das pa sems dang / yid dang
2b4(mdo): dam par shes pa dang / kun gzhi'i spyod yul las yongs su 'das pa/ ye shes dang yid kyi lus su gnas gyur ba/ snyam sa bu dang / dpa' bar 'gro ba dang / chos kyi sprin gyis dang / ti
2b5(mdo): dzin dang ldan pa/ sangs rgyas du mi'i phyag gi dbang bskur bas dbang bskur ba// khams gsum pa'i yul las shin tu 'das pa'i gzhal med khang gi pad mo chen po la 'khod pa rnams dang thabs gcig
2b6(mdo): jugs te/ de na mur 'dug dang / nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ma ba med do// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas mthong / 
2b7(mdo): ba'i chos la bde bar spyad pa/ bdag gi so so rang gi 'phags pa'i ye shes kyis mkhyen pa'i spyod yul btsun par dbyangs 'byin pa sa tshogs kyi gzugs du ma ston pa'i ting nge 'dzin las bzhengs so// bzhengs
2b8(mdo): ma ma sa ni nan can dang/ !wA mas kya yo sa skye/  mas 'i na ma na gag so// dge/ 
3a1(mdo): gzug gi na rgyu ces bya 'ad ba snonakabargyal hA / pa phyogs pasas sa rgya ga
3a2(mdo): da sangs rgyas kyi rgyan gcig dang 'dra bar yongs su snang bar gyur to// mchog phra ba dus kyi phra ba nyid du sangs rgyas kyi ning thams cad kyi nga bzhin tha ba nyid kyang yongs su snang ngo // sings rgya
3a3(mdo): ga sa ma ga ma pa nga gnas so//  na na dang / gas/ tha basmras / 
3a4(mdo): rten cim gas ma rjes kyi da sa // kun du byu napa das pa / rnam dang rtags par shog shA bya ma pa mams dpa man
3a5(mdo): dag dang/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dang/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing gzhad dag na spyod pa byung chub sems dpa' sems dpa 'tshan po rnams kyis gzugs so// de rnam bcom ldan 'das
3a6(mdo): kyis sangs rgyas kyi ning gi rgyan dang / sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa'i mthu phyung ba de dag gzigs nas/ sangs rgyas kyi spyan gyis phyog sa bcur byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor dang bcas pa la
3a7(mdo): gags nas/ byang chub sams dpa sa ma rgya kyi chos thams cad dab pa dgod pa yang dag pa skye ba bzhin du tsun pal mig 'ayul pa/ rnam par dgod pa yang dag pa di stsa ba bzhin du rjon
3b1(mdo): gso rgya zhes bya ba'i sangs rgyas kyi zhi di 'dod pa dang / gzugs dang / gzugs med pa dang / 'du shes med pa'i sems can du gtogs pa'i gzugs srad pa dang / ma rig pa dang / d+hA
3b2(mdo): khri sa she ma ma pas grags na dang/  da kyi la stob sa dang/  pa shes padang /  rkyen padang / 
3b3(mdo): brgyan pa/ gseb med pa/ ring du gnas pa/ zla ba dang / nyi ma dang / nor bu dang / glog dang / 'ja' dang / byi ru dang / bap+pa dang / sdong rom dang / mtshal dang / mgo nag gi 'bru dang / 
3b4(mdo): min drugo sa dang / gse nga/ ma pa kA dang / pad+mod / dung dang /  mgul dang / medangs bu ma me nan na tsug pa'i gzugs pa rnyan pa tho rnam sa ma bag pa med pas spya
3b5(mdo): s+ya ting nge 'dzin la dbang sgyur ba'i phyir smon lam gyi mthar phyin pa bcu'i bsngobs sus thob pa'i byed par can dag sangs rgyas kyi ning stug pa 'ong ngo // de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sangs
3b6(mdo): tsha lam 'a rnas pa dgod pa ya dag pas na du sto mas d+d+he/ thug sa blag pa gcigasag / thub po mas pa rgyangs byanags te/ com ldan nas gdu
3b7(mdo): gcig bcom ldan 'dis kyis bdags cu bathus pa lung bsten pa'i slad du skabs dbya bar gnang na bdag gis du'o// bcom ldan das kyis bags sprul pa/ rnam par dgod pa yang dag pa lta ba bzhin du spyod
4a1(mdo): pa khyod kyis de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i langs rgyas pa dris shig dang / ngas ci dang ci 'dod pa de dang de'i dri ba dris pa lung bstan pas sems mgu
4a2(mdo): bar byas/ khyod kyis ji ltar bzod pa de ltar rlos shig/ de nas pangs rgyar gyi cho thams cad rnam par dgod pa'i rgya na du stod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen no// bcom ldan 'ad
4a3(mdo): kyis skabs phye ba dang / bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das sangs rgyas kyi zhing stug po 'ba' shig 'dod pa dang / gzugs dang / gzugs med pa dang / 'du shes
4a4(mdo): med pa'i sems can las 'das te gnas sam/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing gzhan dag kyang de bzhin nam ci lags/ rigs kyi bu sangs rgyas kyi zhing stug po 'ba' zhig 'dod pa dang / gzugs dang / ga
4a5(mdo): med pa dang / 'du shes med pa'i sems can las 'das te gnam pa ma yin gyi/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing gzhan dag kyang yod do// rigs kyi bu 'di nas pha rol shin tu'ang pha rol sangs rgyas kyi zhing bya ba stong pa
4a6(mdo): brgya 'das pa'i steng gi phyogs chan tshangs pa'i dbyangs de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing dang / de bzhin du sA la'i dbang po'i rgyal po de bzhin gshegs pa
4a7(mdo): dang / skar ba'i rgyal po de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing dang / de bzhin du sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra pa
4a8(mdo): pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi pha rol shin du'ang pha rol tu 'das pa na/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing stong phrag brgya mang po byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi tshogs kyis brgyan pa shin tu
4b1(mdo): yangs shing cha bdag yod de/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das da dag kyang 'khor gyi tshogs de dang dgas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams la bdag gi so so rang gi 'phags pa'i ye shes kyi rtog
4b2(mdo): pa'i spyod yul gyi gtam dang / mthong ba'i chos la bde bar gnas pa'i chos tshig dang / rnam par rtog pa'i spyod yul dang / yi ge dang bral ba/ de bzhin nyid dang / yang dag pa'i mtha' dang / mya ngan
4b3(mdo): las 'odas pa thob par byed pa'i phyi ma'i mtha'i mur gtugs par ston te/ de ni rnam par bkod pa yang dag pa rdo su ba bzhin du ston te/ de ni gang rnam par dgod pa yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du ston pa khyod
4b4(mdo): kyis 'di'i pha rol na 'jig rten gzhan dang sangs rgyas dag yod dam zhes smras pa de'i lan du ngas 'di smras so// rnam par dgod pa yang dag pa ji lta bzhin du ston pa khyod 'ba' shig sangs kyi zhing gi rgyan dang
4b5(mdo): byang chub sems dpa' la ltad mo blta bar 'dod pa'i phyir de bzhin gshegs pa la dri bar sems par mi zad kyi/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shugs 'dzin 'di yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan
4b6(mdo): 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rgyan dang / sangs rgyas kyi sgra'i dbyangs kyi dkyil 'khor dang / spyi gtsug tshad med pa la skad mo blta bar 'dod pa'i phyir sangs rgyas kyi ni dbye ba stong phrag brgya song nas sangs rgyas
4b7(mdo): sangs rgyas kyi gsung gi dbyangs kyi dkyil 'khor ram/ spyi gtsug tshad med pa yang
5a1(mdo): gtsug lta tshad med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa yang dag par rjes su dran ning mi mjed pa 'jig rten gyi khams 'di nyid du byin nas mnyan du yod par sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das tu
5a2(mdo): ma pa dug te/ sa pas nyes par bshags rnas sa sa kyu mas rnamapa pa da ba / mngon pa baspyod na/ bdon ni sbyi lags pa'i ldogs sa tes
5a3(mdo): sangs rgyas kyi zhing stug po nyid du song ste gnas par gyur to// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje'i snying po sa dang sa'i mtshan nyid la mkhas pa
5a4(mdo): sr-i ba dang dmigs su phebs pa dang / rnam par gdon mi ma ba'i gtam zlos pa stan las langs te bla zhes phrag pa gcig lags nas/ pus mo galas pa'i lta ngas la btsugs te/ bcom ldan
5a5(mdo): 'das gangan bde rtsal mo sbyar bas phyag 'tshal te/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas
5a6(mdo): la phyogs gcig cig bcom ldan 'das kyi bdag la nu ba zhus pa lung bstan pa'i slad du skabs dbye bar gnang na bdag gis zlar// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsam pa/ rdo'i snying po khyod kyis/ 
5a7(mdo): dponan gshegs pa dgra tsam pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i mangs rgyas ma dris shig dang / ngas kyid da pa de badres pa nga sbyin pas sems kru bar byag tso kyi
5a8(mdo): //  na sa pa/  da/ bya ba mamadapa' mam dpa' ma thaM com lda kyi pe khyenas/  lda
5b1(mdo): gsal to// bcom ldan 'das sangs rgyas sangs rgyas shes bgyi ba dang / 'chang rgya bar bgyi ba zhes bya ba'i don ci lag sa/ bcom ldan 'das den dam pa 'phags pa'i yumatsham nyid kyi sangs rgyas
5b2(mdo): rigs ston pa 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i spyod pa'i sa la spyod pa dang / gzugs dang / mtshan nyid dang / yang dag par bsdu ba'i lta bar ltung ba rnams dang / mur 'dug gzhan
5b3(mdo): smrab sa mngon par chags pa'i blo'i spyod yul la spyod pa rnams dang / rdul dang / gces pa dang / dbang po dang / phyogs dang / dus dang / na ma mkha' dang / bdag dang / yid dang / dbang
5b4(mdo): don nye bar 'du ba'i lta bar srung po rnams kyi bu rnam par bzlog pa'i slad du bshad du gsol/ bde bar gshegs pa bstan dug sol/ ma rig pa dang / sred pa dang / 
5b5(mdo): thugs dang / snang ba dang / de la skye ba'i yid la byed pa dang / gsum 'du ba'i rnam par rtog pa'i shes pa can dang / rgyu dang / de ma thag pa dang / dbang dang / dmigs pa'i rkyen las byung ba'i rnam par/ 
5b6(mdo): shes pa la chags par spyod pa dang / yod pa dang / med par smra ba'i rtogs pa can dang / chos 'di ba'i phung po dang / gang zag stong pa nyid du lta bar ltung ba rnams kyi yang blo rnam par bzlog pa'i slad du bcom
5b7(mdo): na 'das bstan du gsoso// chos kyi dbang po thos par gyur sa/ bde bar gshegs pa bstan dugasal/ rnam shes lnga nul sogs// mang bdag dam pa ma gtogs par// sa
5b8(mdo): klu nga shes kya dang // deste gang shes 'acang bya zhing // shes bya rnam pa lnga ba rnams// thugs su chud pa sangs rgyar to// chol rnams thams cad sa khyen pa san// byang bdas dang mnyam
6a1(mdo): gshegs pa// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ dge' dgan rdo rje'i snying pos bcu la dbang ba/ rnam par rtag pa'i spyod yul las 'das pa/ mkhas
6a2(mdo): nyid kyi sangs rgyas kyi rigs grags par byed pa dge'o// ral 'bror dam pa sa dbang ba/ sangs rgyas dang 'tshang chu bar yongs su dri 'dri la kyod 'ba'i zhig ltad mo byung ba ma yin gyi/ 
6a3(mdo): ma byed pa bzang po dang / rgyal ba'i bu gzhan dag kyang don 'di la ltad mo bung zhing sangs rgyas kyi dngos po 'dri ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa zhes bya ba'i tshig gi don 'di ci zhag/ ci gzugs de
6a4(mdo): bzhin gshegs pa 'am/ 'on te gzugs las gzhan zhi ba de bzhin gshegs pa 'am/ de bzhin du phung po dang / khams dang / skye mched kyi 'du byed las kyang ste/ nang dang phyi'i mnya
6a5(mdo): pa nyid kyang mi mthong shing byas pa'i rgyu dang 'jig pa'i chos can gyi phyir phung po rnams la de bzhin gshegs pa med de/ rdul phra mo med pa zugs su chung ba'i rgyur shes rang dang / ye shes dang / 
6a6(mdo): de 'dzin gyi spyod yul te/ mnyam par bzhag pa'i thugs kyis yod dgra par rjes su ma gzigs shing phung po rnams gis pa'i phyir de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi sku yin pas na rtag pa / 
6a7(mdo): so// kyo rgyal ba'i bu chos kyi dbyings kyi shin tu phyeb la mkhas pa de ga'// kye rgyal ba'i bu de bsan dge bzhin du nyon de yidas gyis shig dang ngas khyod la shad do// bcom
6a8(mdo): 'das dga'i nas nas byang chub sems dpa' sem sa dpa' che na du'i gang po bcom ldan 'das las kyi phyin to// bcom ldan 'das kyis de la bka' la pa/ rigs kyi 'do
6b1(mdo): rnams ni mnobasam med pa'i phyir te/ de bzhin gshegs pa ni 'di rnams las rang ma thar yang skye lta'o// gzugs spyod pa med cing sems med pa ste/ 'thung ba med pa tshas cam
6b2(mdo): rig pa/ rdza dang shing dang thong dro dang 'dra ba/ shin tu phra ba'i dus kyi tshogs dbu' dang 'dra ba'o// tshor ba ni gnyis chags pa las chu'i chu bur dang 'dra bar bya'o// 'du shes ni bupa pa dang / 
6b3(mdo): pan la rdzogs pa'i rgyalas zung ste// de yang gi nyis las rgyas pa'i sdug tu drug te/ dab nga byed kyis mngon pa gsus pa'i sam nya byed par 'bab chen
6b4(mdo): rnams cu'i rnabasas par ma' dgas dang sa ma pa dam ma tshur mongs pa mangs par byed do// de bzhin du ga shA nyid ma na
6b5(mdo): bdag nyid ma yin pa'i gzugs su 'jug pa/ yang dag pa ma ldan pa yongs su brtags pa las skyesas+ho/ dpyod pa dmas kyis brjod pa las migs shig tu mi dmigs pa/ 'od
6b6(mdo): da / shas ma mdun /  kyil ga //  malamanag kyi 'dun pa yang sa chag
7a1(mdo): padang / rdung zad 'byung po yang dmigs su med do// de bzhin du mi shes pas phogapan bud med dang skyes pa sa sogs pa mthong ba yang mngon par sangs rgyas na mi
7a2(mdo): 'du byed rnams ni dra shing gi snying po lta bu ste bcol na/ lus dang dge dang yid las byung ba gzugs med pa rnams rnal 'byor can gyi dpyod pa pa rnams kyis mi rnyed do// rnam par
7a3(mdo): shes pa ni sgyu ma lte bu de'i bdag nyid med pa ste/ zlu ma byed pa 'am/ de'i slob mas nan tan du rtswa dang shing dang byeng rdo tsam la brten te gzugs kyi yan lag du ma las mngon par bsgrub
7a4(mdo): pa'i sgyu ma'i gzugs glang po dang / rta dang / shing rta dang / mi dang / rgyan ma brtags pa'i gzugs kyi phyogs gcig ngo mtshar du bstan pa lta bu dang / gzhan yang mkhas
7a5(mdo): rnamase la ma yin gyi bus pa'i 'gro ba rnams la 'drin pa de bzhin du rnam par shes pa yang rnam pa gzhan du 'dug la/ rnam pa gzhan du shin du brtags shing shin tu rtog ste
7a6(mdo): de yang bdag bdag la 'dzin pa gnyis su shes nas/ sgyums mngon par grub pa'i gzugs gcig po'i ngo mtshar dang 'dra bar phyir ldog go// de bzhin gshegs pa ni rtag pa ba
7a7(mdo): pa ther zug mi 'jig pa ste/ sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa bsgom pa'i rnal 'byor can rnams kyi
7a8(mdo): dbyis dang / nam / byangamal kyi mnags na sa dang / zung ba dang / 'byung ba'i mas rgyas bcom ldanas
7b1(mdo): rnams kyis bstan te/ 'di ltar de bzhin gshegs pa rnams byung yang rung / mabyung yang rung / chos rnams kyi chos nyid chos kyi gnas nyid dang / chos gyi dbyings dang / chos sngon med pa gnyis
7b2(mdo): 'di ni de bzhin gnas pa'o// rdo rje'i snying po ston med pa zhes bya ba ni yang 'byung ba'i nyes pa thams cad dang bral ba 'o// rdo rje'i snying po skyon med pa ni nyes pa thams cad dang bral bar ma zad
7b3(mdo): skyon med par 'da' ba ni byang chub sems dpas spang bar bya ste/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar ting nge 'dzin gyi sgo de nyid du myos te/ sems can la lta ba med par gyur cing yang dag tu
7b4(mdo): mtha' mngon du byas nas lcags bsreg pa'i mo dang 'dra bar mya ngan las 'da' ba 'gyur te/ rnamams can gyi dgos pa la brtson 'grus bting zhing snying rje chen po dang / pha rol tu phyin pa rnams dang tha
7b5(mdo): sa sangs rgyas kyi gdung rnam par chad par byed cing nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas mur 'dug byed pa'i lam du 'gro ste/ ting nge 'dzin gyi 'dam du glang po chen po 'dra bar rnam par thogs te/ rnam par
7b6(mdo): shes pa'i yul rab tu zhum pas sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi skye mched thams cad kyis kun nas ma gnas shing rdzogs par mi byed par 'gyur ba'i phyir mngon du mi bya zhing / ma rig pa dang / 
7b7(mdo): par gnas par bya'o// de ltar sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi sku'i rjes su zhugs te sangs rgyas kyi che ba nyid shes pas chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i sangs rgyas rnam pa sna tshogs kyi tshul gyi yul la nye bar
7b8(mdo): spyod pa/ sprul pa'i yul can/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyis ting nge 'dzin pa
8a1(mdo): che ba nyid myong nas de bzhin gshegs pa bdag gi so so rang gis rig pa 'phags pa'i ye shes kyis rtogs pa'i spyod yul gyi sar zhugs te/ thams cad du 'gro ba ma g.yos
8a2(mdo): / stosnyo par 'gyur te/ gnas gyur pa/ yid bzhin gyi ye shes dang ting nge 'dzin can/ stobs dang / mngon par shes pa dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa dang / dbang la spyod pa/ rang pa'i rgyal po
8a3(mdo): dang 'dra bar ma zhugs pa'i chu bo zla ba lnga zur 'gro ste/ blta ba'i don yod pa/ mi'i bdag po thams cad kyi tshogs kyi 'khor du sems can rnams kyi bsam pa ji lta bar 'dod pa'i gzugs dag
8a4(mdo): sa sangs rgyas kyi phreng stug po bstan pa'i phyir sems can gyi bsam pa bzhin du 'jug par 'gyur ro// 'dod pa'i khams kyi dbang po thams cad dang / dbang skur ba'i byang chub sems dpa' sems
8a5(mdo): dpa' chen po nor tshun pa che'i snying po la sogs pa'i gnas dag tu bde ba rnams myong bar byas te sa'i rim pa rnams bskrun nas zhing nas zhing du phun sum bod pa rnams rab tu skyon cing dri ma
8a6(mdo): mthar thug par thasdu pa grub pa'i sngags 'chang ltar mi snang zhing khang khyim gyi lha ltar don gnas bzhin du ma snang ba'i gzugs su kyis ni 'dug pa ltar de dge sprul pa'i 'di zer dang / 
8a7(mdo): pas sprul pa la spyod cing 'gro'o// song nas kyang de bzhin gshegs bI sprul pa'i munub ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku la zhen nas gnas par 'gyur ro// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyi
8b1(mdo): tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag gsungs so// dbang po phung po sprul yin te// sred dang ma rig las kyang yin/ 
8b2(mdo): 'dod chags rnams// zhags pa sems paskyed de yin no// khro ba me lce mnyam pa ste// zhe sdang drug gi dngos po yin// brub spyod rnal 'byor bzang can gyis// 'di dag rtag tu rnam gzhigs te/ 
8b3(mdo): po rnam sa ni dor ban phyir// rnal 'byor can gyis rnal nastor spyod// gzugs ni 'byung ba'i tshogs yin te// srung po lhag mi gzugs med pa// de bzhin par snang mo dang // grib la rjo
8b4(mdo): la sogs med// mkha' la rlung gzugs mi snang dang // bya yi rjes rnams ji bzhin no// mkhas pas so so rang rig pa// yang dag nyid dang yang dag mtha'// tshig gi spyod yul 'das pa ni/
